<!-- OneTrust -->
    <script>
      document.cookie.split(";").forEach(cookie => {
        const name = cookie.split("=")[0].trim();
        if (
          name === "OptanonConsent" &&
          cookie.indexOf("&version=6.23.0&") >= 0
        ) {
          const functionalityConsentSet = cookie.indexOf("C0003") >= 0;
          if (!functionalityConsentSet) {
            const encodedColon = encodeURIComponent(":");
            const analyticsConsentGranted =
              cookie.indexOf(`C0002${encodedColon}1`) >= 0;
            const adsConsentGranted =
              cookie.indexOf(`C0004${encodedColon}1`) >= 0;
            if (analyticsConsentGranted || adsConsentGranted) {
              cookie = cookie.replace(
                "groups=",
                `groups=C0003${encodedColon}1,`,
              );

// Intentionally leave off the expiration such that this becomes a session cookie
              cookie =
                cookie + "; path=/; domain=www.crunchbase.com; Samesite=Lax;";
              document.cookie = cookie;
            }
          }
        }
      });
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
      window["GroupsUpdatedHistory"] = window["GroupsUpdatedHistory"] || [];
      window.addEventListener("OneTrustGroupsUpdated", event => {
        window["GroupsUpdatedHistory"].push(event);

_ngcontent-ng-c3434966195="" class="summary ng-star-inserted"><div _ngcontent-ng-c3434966195="" class="summary-title"> Summary </div><div _ngcontent-ng-c3434966195="" class="summary-content" style="-webkit-line-clamp: 2;"> SpaceX has been actively involved in various growth activities. The company has been expanding its operations in Texas, as indicated by its plans to make Starbase an official city and its role in regional growth. SpaceX has also been increasing its dominance in U.S. launch contracts and has launched multiple Starlink satellites, further expanding its global internet coverage. Additionally, SpaceX's valuation has reached $350 billion, making it the world's most valuable startup.
